"Camille Jouvenceau, who lives in the Arve Valley in France, has been suffering from bronchitis, asthma and ear infections since the end of November due to the high levels of fine and ultra-fine particle pollution in the area. The air is often cooler in the valley, which prevents it from rising or dispersing easily, and the mountains block the wind.
